<link rel="schema.DC" href="http://purl.org/DC/elements/1.0/" /><meta name="dc.Title" content="Dutch courage? Effects of acute alcohol consumption on self-ratings and observer ratings of foreign language skills" /><meta name="citation_journal_title" content="Journal of Psychopharmacology" /><meta name="dc.Creator" content="Fritz Renner" /><meta name="dc.Creator" content="Inge Kersbergen" /><meta name="dc.Creator" content="Matt Field" /><meta name="dc.Creator" content="Jessica Werthmann" /><meta name="dc.Subject" content="Acute alcohol consumption; executive functioning; popular beliefs" /><meta name="dc.Description" content="Aims:A popular belief is that alcohol improves the ability to speak in a foreign language. The effect of acute alcohol consumption on perceived foreign language performance and actual foreign language performance in foreign language learners has not been investigated. The aim of the current study was to test the effects of acute alcohol consumption on self-rated and observer-rated verbal foreign language performance in participants who have recently learned this language.Methods:Fifty native German speakers who had recently learned Dutch were randomized to receive either a low dose of alcohol or a control beverage that contained no alcohol. Following the experimental manipulation, participants took part in a standardized discussion in Dutch with a blinded experimenter. The discussion was audio-recorded and foreign language skills were subsequently rated by two native Dutch speakers who were blind to the experimental condition (observer-rating). Participants also rated their own individual Dutch language s..." /><meta name="dc.Publisher" content="SAGE PublicationsSage UK: London, England" /><meta name="dc.Date" scheme="WTN8601" content="2017-10-18" /><meta name="dc.Type" content="research-article" /><meta name="dc.Format" content="text/HTML" /><meta name="dc.Identifier" scheme="doi" content="10.1177/0269881117735687" /><meta name="dc.Identifier" scheme="publisher-id" content="10.1177_0269881117735687" /><meta name="dc.Source" content="https://doi.org/10.1177/0269881117735687" /><meta name="dc.Language" content="en" /><meta name="dc.Coverage" content="Sage UK: London, England" /><meta name="keywords" content="Acute alcohol consumption, executive functioning, popular beliefs" />

        <div class="wrapped " id='mobileQuickSearch'>
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><util:actionContext/>











        
    



<div class="quickSearchFormContainer">
    

    <form action="/action/doSearch" id="quickSearch" name="quickSearch" class="quickSearchForm " style="padding-left: 0px" title="Quick Search" method="get"><span class="simpleSearchBoxContainer" id="meme">
                    
                    

                    
                     
                             <input name="AllField" class="searchText main-search-field autocomplete" value=""
                                    type="search" id="searchText" title="Type search term here" placeholder="Search: keywords, title, authors, DOI" autocomplete="off"
                                    data-history-items-conf="3"
                                    data-publication-titles-conf="3"
                                    data-topics-conf="3"
                                    data-contributors-conf="3">
                         
                </span>
                
            
        

        
            




<input class="mainSearchButton searchButtons pointer" title="search" type="submit" value="Search" /></form>

<script>
    if (true) {
        $(document).ready(function () {

            /* For Minimize  the Screen and Mobile Support */
            $(window).resize(function() {
                $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete( "search" );
            });


            $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete({
                minLength: 0,
                source: [],
                select: AutoCompleteSelectHandler,
                open: function (event, ui) {

                    var currentWidth = $(this).outerWidth();
                    var iconSpan = 30;
                    if (currentWidth < 200) {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+4) + iconSpan

                        });
                    } else {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+40) + iconSpan

                        });
                    }
                    $("ul.ui-autocomplete li a").each(function () {
                        var currentValue = $(this).html();
                        if(currentValue) {
                            var lastIndex = currentValue.lastIndexOf(",")
                            var currentInput = currentValue.substring(0, lastIndex);
                            var ourOptions = currentValue.substring(lastIndex + 1);
                            $(this).html("<span style=\"position: relative;top: 5px\"><img src=\"/templates/jsp/_style2/_sage/images/quick-search-icon.png\" /></span>" + "<b>" + " " + currentInput + "</b>" + ourOptions);
                        }
                    });
                },
                focus: function (event, ui) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                },
                response: function (event, ui) {


                    var value = $(this).val();

                    if (value.length != 0)
                    {
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value+ ', in This journal',
                            'value': 'This journal'
                        });
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value + ', in All SAGE journals',
                            'value': 'All SAGE journals'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });



            /* Get slected Option from autoComplete*/
            function AutoCompleteSelectHandler(event, ui) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var selectedObj = ui.item;
                var value = selectedObj.value;
                var currentValue = $(this).val();
                $("input[name=AllField]").val(currentValue);

                if (value == 'This journal') {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                } else {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                }

            }


            /* when click Enter */
            $(".searchText").on("keydown", function (event) {
                if (event.which == 13){
                    var selectedValue = $(this).val();
                    if (selectedValue == 'This journal') {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                    } else {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                    }
                }

            });


        })
    }

</script></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <form action="/action/doSearch" id="quickSearch" name="quickSearch" class="quickSearchForm " style="padding-left: 0px" title="Quick Search" method="get"><span class="simpleSearchBoxContainer" id="meme">

                                    data-history-items-conf="3"
                                    data-publication-titles-conf="3"
                                    data-topics-conf="3"

<script>
    if (true) {
        $(document).ready(function () {

            /* For Minimize  the Screen and Mobile Support */
            $(window).resize(function() {
                $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete( "search" );
            });


            $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete({
                minLength: 0,
                source: [],
                select: AutoCompleteSelectHandler,
                open: function (event, ui) {

                    var currentWidth = $(this).outerWidth();
                    var iconSpan = 30;
                    if (currentWidth < 200) {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+4) + iconSpan

                        });
                    } else {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+40) + iconSpan

                        });
                    }
                    $("ul.ui-autocomplete li a").each(function () {
                        var currentValue = $(this).html();
                        if(currentValue) {
                            var lastIndex = currentValue.lastIndexOf(",")
                            var currentInput = currentValue.substring(0, lastIndex);
                            var ourOptions = currentValue.substring(lastIndex + 1);
                            $(this).html("<span style=\"position: relative;top: 5px\"><img src=\"/templates/jsp/_style2/_sage/images/quick-search-icon.png\" /></span>" + "<b>" + " " + currentInput + "</b>" + ourOptions);
                        }
                    });
                },
                focus: function (event, ui) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                },
                response: function (event, ui) {


                    var value = $(this).val();

                    if (value.length != 0)
                    {
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value+ ', in This journal',
                            'value': 'This journal'
                        });
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value + ', in All SAGE journals',
                            'value': 'All SAGE journals'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });



            /* Get slected Option from autoComplete*/
            function AutoCompleteSelectHandler(event, ui) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var selectedObj = ui.item;
                var value = selectedObj.value;
                var currentValue = $(this).val();
                $("input[name=AllField]").val(currentValue);

                if (value == 'This journal') {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                } else {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                }

            }


            /* when click Enter */
            $(".searchText").on("keydown", function (event) {
                if (event.which == 13){
                    var selectedValue = $(this).val();
                    if (selectedValue == 'This journal') {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                    } else {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                    }
                }

            });


        })
    }

</script></div>
        </div>
    </div>

        <div class="wrapped " id='portalMobileLogin'>
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><div data-pb-dropzone="contents">
    


    
    
    
    
    
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
            
                
            
            
                
                
                
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
            
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
    
    

    
    <div class="widget general-html-asset none  widget-none  widget-compact-all" id="66fe8e60-9b5c-42dc-b5da-3aff92108756"  >
        
        

        <div class="wrapped " >
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><script>


function panelToggle(panelIdString, closePanel1String, closePanel2String) {
	
	if (panelIdString) {	
		var panelId = document.getElementById(panelIdString);
		var panelDisplay = window.getComputedStyle(panelId, null).getPropertyValue('display');

		if (panelDisplay === 'none' || panelDisplay === '') {
			panelId.style.display = 'block';
		} else {
			panelId.style.display = 'none';
		}
	}
  
	if (closePanel1String) {
		var closePanel1Id = document.getElementById(closePanel1String);

		closePanel1Id.style.display = 'none';
	}

	if (closePanel2String) {
		var closePanel2Id = document.getElementById(closePanel2String);

		closePanel2Id.style.display = 'none';
	}
}

function panelToggleFixed(panelIdStrings, panelClassString) {
	var panelIds=panelIdStrings.split(',');
	var panelIdString;
	//console.log(panelIds);
	for (i=0; i<panelIds.length; i++) {
		try {
			//console.log("Attempting to toggle "+panelIds[i]);
			panelToggle(panelIds[i]);
			panelIdString=panelIds[i];
			break;
		}
		catch (x){
			//console.log("Caught Exception in toggling "+panelIds[i]);
		}
	}
	if (panelIdString) {	
		var $panelId = $('#' + panelIdString);
		if ($panelId) {
			var panelDisplay = window.getComputedStyle($panelId[0], null).getPropertyValue('display');

			if (panelDisplay === 'none' || panelDisplay === '') {
				$panelId.find("." + panelClassString).removeClass("fixedPanel");
			} else {
				$panelId.find("." + panelClassString).addClass("fixedPanel");
			}
		}
	}
	else {
		console.log("No panel found to attach class "+panelClassString);
	}
}

function closeSlidePanel (closePanelString) {
		var closePanelId = document.getElementById(closePanelString);
		var panelLeft = window.getComputedStyle(closePanelId, null).getPropertyValue('left');
		var panelWidth = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(closePanelId, null).getPropertyValue('width'));
		var panelPaddingLeft = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(closePanelId, null).getPropertyValue('padding-left'));
		var panelOffset = panelWidth + panelPaddingLeft;

		closePanelId.style.left = "-"+String(panelOffset)+"px";
}

/* Toggle the opening or closing of a slider panel, and closes additional panels*/
function panelSlide(panelIdString, closePanel1String, closePanel2String) {
	
	if (panelIdString) {
		var panelId = document.getElementById(panelIdString);
		var panelLeft = window.getComputedStyle(panelId, null).getPropertyValue('left');

		if (panelLeft === "0px" || panelLeft === "") {
			closeSlidePanel (panelIdString);
		} else {
			panelId.style.left = "0";
		}
	}
  
	if (closePanel1String) {
		closeSlidePanel (closePanel1String);
	}
  
	if (closePanel2String) {
		closeSlidePanel (closePanel2String);
	}
}

function portalInstitutionalLoginToggle() {
  var myInstitutionalLoginId = document.getElementById('portalInstitutionalLogin');

  if (myInstitutionalLoginId.style.display === 'none' || myInstitutionalLoginId.style.display === '') {
    myInstitutionalLoginId.style.display = 'block';
  } else {
    myInstitutionalLoginId.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

function mobileMenuSlide(menuIdString, closeMenuIdString) {

  var menuBottom = $(menuIdString).css("bottom");
 
   if (menuBottom === "-1000px" || menuBottom === "") {

	var menuHeight = $(menuIdString).height();
	var menuPaddingBottom = 47;
	var menuOffset = menuHeight + menuPaddingBottom;
 
	$(menuIdString).css({"bottom":menuPaddingBottom+"px"});
  } else {
	closeMobileMenu (menuIdString);
  }
  if (closeMenuIdString) {
	closeMobileMenu (closeMenuIdString);
  }
}

function closeMobileMenu (closeMenuIdString) {
	$(closeMenuIdString).css({"bottom":"-1000px"});
}

function portalLoginSetup() {
	$("#portalLoginBar .loginBar > a:nth-child(1)").attr("href", "#");
	$("#portalLoginBar #indivLogin").attr("href", "#");

	if ($("#myAccountLoginPanel .loginForm td").hasClass("error")) {
		if ($(".portalHeaderMobile").css("display")!="none") {
			portalMobileLoginDisplay();
		}
		panelToggle('myAccountLoginPanel');
	} 
}

function portalMobileMenusDisplay() {
	panelSlide("portalMobileMenus", "portalMobileLogin");
	panelToggle("portalMobileMenusOverlay", "mobileQuickSearch", "portalMobileLoginOverlay");
}

function portalMobileLoginDisplay() {
	console.log("portalMobileLoginDisplay");
	panelSlide("portalMobileLogin", "portalMobileMenus");
	panelToggle("portalMobileLoginOverlay", "mobileQuickSearch", "portalMobileMenusOverlay");
}

function portalMobileSearchDisplay() {
	panelSlide("", "portalMobileLogin", "portalMobileMenus");
	panelToggle("mobileQuickSearch", "portalMobileMenusOverlay", "portalMobileLoginOverlay");
}

var panelOpenning=false; // Flag for omitting click event while openning the panel

$(document).ready(function () {
	portalLoginSetup ();

	$(document).click(function(event) { 
		if (!panelOpenning) {
			if($(event.target).closest('#portalAccountPanel').length==0 && $('#portalAccountPanel').is(":visible")) {
				$('#portalAccountPanel').fadeOut('fast'); // user clicked outside of panel --> close panel
			}
			if($(event.target).closest('#myAccountLoginPanel').length==0 && $('#myAccountLoginPanel').is(":visible")) {
				$('#myAccountLoginPanel').fadeOut('fast'); // user clicked outside of panel --> close panel
			}
		}
		else {
			panelOpenning = false;
		}
	});
	
	$(document).keyup(function(event) {
		if (event.keyCode == 27) { // escape key maps to keycode `27`
			if($('#portalAccountPanel').is(":visible")) {
				$('#portalAccountPanel').fadeOut('fast'); 
			}
			if($('#myAccountLoginPanel').is(":visible")) {
				$('#myAccountLoginPanel').fadeOut('fast');
			}
		}
	});
	$("#portalLoginBar .loginBar > a:nth-child(1)").click(function(event) { 
		panelToggle('myAccountLoginPanel', 'portalInstitutionalLogin');
		panelOpenning = true;
		event.preventDefault();
	});

	$("#portalLoginBar #indivLogin").click(function(event) {
		panelToggle('portalAccountPanel', 'portalInstitutionalLogin');
		panelOpenning = true;
		event.preventDefault();
	});

	$("#portalMobileLoginOverlay").click(function(event) { 
		portalMobileLoginDisplay();
		panelOpenning = false; // this should trigger closing of panel, as well.
		event.preventDefault();
	});
	
	// When the user clicks on <span> (x):
	$(".closeMenuButton").click(function(event){ 
		portalMobileLoginDisplay();
		panelOpenning = false; // this should trigger closing of panel, as well.
		event.preventDefault();
	});
});


</script>
<div id="portalMobileLoginOverlay"></div></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="widget general-html-asset none doNotShow widget-none" id="44725496-ccc2-4bc2-a774-8ef7333d50af"  >
        
        

        <div class="wrapped " >
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none "><script type="text/javascript">

function offset(el) {
    var rect = el.getBoundingClientRect(),
    scrollLeft = window.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft,
    scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    return { top: rect.top + scrollTop, left: rect.left + scrollLeft, bottom: rect.bottom + scrollTop , right: rect.right + scrollLeft }
}

var myScrollFunc = function() {
  var y = window.pageYOffset;
  var $quickSearchId = $("#journalQuickSearch").parent();

  if (y >= offset(document.getElementById("portalQuickSearch")).bottom) {
    $quickSearchId.removeClass("doNotShow");
  } else {
    $quickSearchId.addClass("doNotShow");
  }
};

window.addEventListener("scroll", myScrollFunc); 

$(window).bind('orientationchange', function(event) {
  $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete('close');
});

$(window).scroll(function(){
  var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
  if(scroll>1)
    $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete('close');
 });

<script type="text/javascript">
/* (start) NK 20170526 [Hijacking this to temporarily fix LIT-161503] */
// Handle trailing commas dynamically
$(document).ready(function(){  
    var onlyCommas = $(".authors .hlFld-ContribAuthor span.NLM_contrib-group").text().split(' ').join('').split(',').join('')==="";
    if (onlyCommas) {
		$(".authors .hlFld-ContribAuthor span.NLM_contrib-group").css({"display":"none"});
    }
});

// Fix missing link 'Show all authors'
$(document).ready(function(){
    var $root = $('.author-container');
    var $exp = $root.find('.hlFld-ContribAuthor');
    if ($exp.size() > 0) {
        var $contr = $exp.find('.contribDegrees');
        if ($contr.size() > 3) {
			$('a.show-all-link.js__toggleArticleAuthors').css({"display":"block"});
		}
	}
});

// Add arrow indicator next to author expander [SAGE-1411]
$(document).ready(function() {
    var $root = $('.author-container');
    var $exp = $root.find('.hlFld-ContribAuthor');
    if ($exp.size() > 0) {
        var $contr = $exp.find('.contribDegrees');
        if ($contr.size() > 3) {
			$('span.expandable-author').before('<span id="expandableAuthorArrow" class="arrow-down indicator"></span>');
			//$('span.expandable-author').attr( 'tabIndex', 0 ); // add it in tabIndex for keyboard navigability
		
			$('span.expandable-author').click(function() {
				if ($(this).text()==="Show all authors") {
					$("#expandableAuthorArrow").toggleClass('arrow-down arrow-up');
				}
				else {
					$("#expandableAuthorArrow").toggleClass('arrow-up arrow-down');
				}
			});
		}
		else {
			$exp.find('span.more-than').remove();
		}
	}
});


// Remove content outside of tags
function sanitizeDiv($root) { 
	var $commas=$root.contents(":not(span.contribDegrees):not(.expandable-author):not(span.more-than)");
	var $source = $root.html();
	//console.log($source);
	$root[0].innerHTML=$source.replace($commas.text(), " ");
}


// Fix multi contrib-group case 
$(function () {
	var $authorsList= $('.publicationContentAuthors'); // Limit changes inside authors only (not Article Information)
    var $root = $authorsList.find('.hlFld-ContribAuthor');
	if ($root.size()>0) {
		var $exp = $root.find('.expandable-author');
		if ($exp.size() > 1) {
			var $contr = $root.find('span.contribDegrees');
			$root.find('.more-than').remove(); //if >3 authors, this will be added explictly, else it is not needed.
			$root.find('span.expandable-author').remove();
			if ($contr.size() > 3) {
				// create new element for .expandable-author and move everything in it
				// do not add the class yet - it would be removed
				//var $ea = $('<div/>').appendTo($root).append($root.find('.expandable-author *, span.contribDegrees'));
				var $ea = $('<div/>').appendTo($root).append($root.find('span.contribDegrees'));
				$root.find('.expandable-author').remove();
				$ea.addClass('expandable-author');
				// move first 3 authors out of the .expandable-author
				$root.prepend($ea.find('span.contribDegrees').slice(0,3)).append('<span class="more-than">...</span>');
			}
			else {
				$root.find('.expandable-author').remove();
			}
			// Fix missing punctuation
			$root.find('span.contribDegrees').each(function(){
				if (this.nextSibling && this.nextSibling.nodeType === Node.ELEMENT_NODE) {
					var $e = $(this);
					var t = $e.text().trim();
					var i = t.lastIndexOf(',');
					if (t.length>0 && i < t.length-1){
						$e.append(", ");
					}
				}
			})
		}
		sanitizeDiv($root);
	}
});
/*(end) NK 20170526 [Hijacking this to temporarily fix LIT-161503] */

<script>
    if (true) {
        $(document).ready(function () {

            /* For Minimize  the Screen and Mobile Support */
            $(window).resize(function() {
                $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete( "search" );
            });


            $('input[name=AllField]').autocomplete({
                minLength: 0,
                source: [],
                select: AutoCompleteSelectHandler,
                open: function (event, ui) {

                    var currentWidth = $(this).outerWidth();
                    var iconSpan = 30;
                    if (currentWidth < 200) {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+4) + iconSpan

                        });
                    } else {
                        $(this).autocomplete("widget").css({
                            "width": (currentWidth+40) + iconSpan

                        });
                    }
                    $("ul.ui-autocomplete li a").each(function () {
                        var currentValue = $(this).html();
                        if(currentValue) {
                            var lastIndex = currentValue.lastIndexOf(",")
                            var currentInput = currentValue.substring(0, lastIndex);
                            var ourOptions = currentValue.substring(lastIndex + 1);
                            $(this).html("<span style=\"position: relative;top: 5px\"><img src=\"/templates/jsp/_style2/_sage/images/quick-search-icon.png\" /></span>" + "<b>" + " " + currentInput + "</b>" + ourOptions);
                        }
                    });
                },
                focus: function (event, ui) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                },
                response: function (event, ui) {


                    var value = $(this).val();

                    if (value.length != 0)
                    {
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value+ ', in This journal',
                            'value': 'This journal'
                        });
                        ui.content.push({
                            'label': value + ', in All SAGE journals',
                            'value': 'All SAGE journals'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });



            /* Get slected Option from autoComplete*/
            function AutoCompleteSelectHandler(event, ui) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var selectedObj = ui.item;
                var value = selectedObj.value;
                var currentValue = $(this).val();
                $("input[name=AllField]").val(currentValue);

                if (value == 'This journal') {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                } else {
                    $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                }

            }


            /* when click Enter */
            $(".searchText").on("keydown", function (event) {
                if (event.which == 13){
                    var selectedValue = $(this).val();
                    if (selectedValue == 'This journal') {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').append("<input type='hidden' name='SeriesKey' value='jopa'>").submit();
                    } else {
                        $(this).closest('#quickSearch').submit();
                    }
                }

            });


        })
    }

function genSide(part, dbid, linkoutUrl, display, doi, url, citNum, value) {
    if (dbid != anyDbId && (140737488355327 & dbid) == 0) return;
    var content = sideParts[part];
    if (linkoutUrl) { content = content.replace(/{\$linkoutUrl}/g, linkoutUrl); }
    if (display) { content = content.replace(/{\$display}/g, display); }
    if (doi) { content = content.replace(/{\$doi}/g, doi); }
    if (url) {
        content = content.replace(/{\$url}/g, url);
        content = content.replace(/{\$urlEnc}/g, encodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(url)));
    }
    if (citNum) { content = content.replace(/{\$citNum}/g, citNum); }
    if (value) { content = content.replace(/{\$value}/g, value); }
    document.write(content);
}

function genRefLink(dbid, id, key, textOfLink) {
    if (140737488355327 & dbid != 0) {
        if (typeof textOfLink === "undefined") {
            if (sfxRefDisplay[dbid].substring(0,1) == "[") {
                textOfLink = sfxRefDisplay[dbid];
            } else {
                textOfLink = "["+sfxRefDisplay[dbid]+"]";
            }
            // ToDo: move '[' and ']' to sfxRefDisplay (UPDATE: finish changing sfxRefDisplays and remove this branch)
        }
        else{ textOfLink = unescape(textOfLink)};

        if(document.disableRefLinkWrite == null){
            document.write("<a class='ref' href=\"javascript:popRefLink("+dbid+",'"+id+"','"+key+"')\">"+textOfLink+"<\/a>");
        }
    }
}

    if (! ptype) { ptype = ""; }
    var pt = rid.charAt(0) + "0269881117735687" + ptype;
    return popupRef(citart, rid, doi, pt, area, width, height);

function articleInfoToggle() {
  var articleInfoID = document.getElementById('articleInfo');
  if (articleInfoID.style.display === 'none' || articleInfoID.style.display === '') {
    articleInfoID.style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById("authorInfoArrow").className="arrow-up indicator";
  } else {
    articleInfoID.style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById("authorInfoArrow").className="arrow-down indicator";
  }
  return false;
}

function articleInfoToggleMobile() {
  var articleInfoID = document.getElementById('articleInfo');
  if (articleInfoID.style.display === 'none' || articleInfoID.style.display === '') {
    articleInfoID.style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById("authorInfoImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/Cross-blue-grey.png";
  } else {
    articleInfoID.style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById("authorInfoImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/author-info.png";
  }
}
</script>

                <article class="article">
                    
                            <!-- abstract content --><div class="hlFld-Abstract"><a name="abstract"></a><div class="sectionInfo abstractSectionHeading"><h2 class="sectionHeading">Abstract</h2></div><div class="abstractSection abstractInFull"><div id="section1-0269881117735687" class="NLM_sec NLM_sec_level_1"><a name="_i1"><!--title--></a><div class="sectionInfo"><h2 class="sectionHeading">Aims:</h2><div class="sectionJumpTo"></div></div><p>A popular belief is that alcohol improves the ability to speak in a foreign language. The effect of acute alcohol consumption on perceived foreign language performance and actual foreign language performance in foreign language learners has not been investigated. The aim of the current study was to test the effects of acute alcohol consumption on self-rated and observer-rated verbal foreign language performance in participants who have recently learned this language.</p></div><div id="section2-0269881117735687" class="NLM_sec NLM_sec_level_1"><a name="_i2"><!--title--></a><div class="sectionInfo"><h2 class="sectionHeading">Methods:</h2><div class="sectionJumpTo"></div></div><p>Fifty native German speakers who had recently learned Dutch were randomized to receive either a low dose of alcohol or a control beverage that contained no alcohol. Following the experimental manipulation, participants took part in a standardized discussion in Dutch with a blinded experimenter. The discussion was audio-recorded and foreign language skills were subsequently rated by two native Dutch speakers who were blind to the experimental condition (observer-rating). Participants also rated their own individual Dutch language skills during the discussion (self-rating).</p></div><div id="section3-0269881117735687" class="NLM_sec NLM_sec_level_1"><a name="_i3"><!--title--></a><div class="sectionInfo"><h2 class="sectionHeading">Results:</h2><div class="sectionJumpTo"></div></div><p>Participants who consumed alcohol had significantly better observer-ratings for their Dutch language, specifically better pronunciation, compared with those who did not consume alcohol. However, alcohol had no effect on self-ratings of Dutch language skills.</p></div><div id="section4-0269881117735687" class="NLM_sec NLM_sec_level_1"><a name="_i4"><!--title--></a><div class="sectionInfo"><h2 class="sectionHeading">Conclusions:</h2><div class="sectionJumpTo"></div></div><p>Acute alcohol consumption may have beneficial effects on the pronunciation of a foreign language in people who have recently learned that language.</p></div></div></div><!-- /abstract content --><a name="_i32"><!--title--></a><div class="sectionInfo"><h2 class="sectionHeading">References</h2><div class="sectionJumpTo"><div class="sectionLabel">Section:</div><form style="margin-bottom:0"><select name="select23" class="fulltextdd" onChange="GoTo(this, 'self')"><option value="#" selected="#">Choose</option><option value="#">Top of page</option><option value="#abstract">Abstract</option><option value="#_i5">Introduction</option><option value="#_i6">Method</option><option value="#_i29">Discussion</option><option value="#_i31">Conclusions</option><option value="">References &lt;&lt;</option></select></form><div class="nextPrevSec"><a href="#_i31" class="up"><img src="/templates/jsp/images/arrow_up.gif" width="11" height="9" border="0" hspace="5" alt="Previous section" /></a></div></div></div><table border="0" class="references"><tr id="bibr1-0269881117735687"><td class="refnumber"> </td><td valign="top">

    <div class="widget general-html-asset none  widget-none  widget-compact-all" id="a45164ee-0c62-411e-8fa7-de8c91dcd599"  >
        
        

        <div class="wrapped " >
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><script type="text/javascript">
    var mobileBreakpoint = 768;
    var tabletBreakpoint = 1025;
    // This file contains the functions to control responsive bahaviour of some site items
    function setMobileLabels() {
        $("#journalHomeMenuItem").text("Journal Home");
        $("#journalSubscribeLink").text("Subscribe to this Journal");
        $("#journalAboutMenuItem").text("About this Journal");
        $("#portalBrowseLink").text("Browse Journals");
    };

    function setDesktopLabels() {
        $("#journalHomeMenuItem").text("Home");
        $("#journalSubscribeLink").text("Subscribe");
        $("#journalAboutMenuItem").text("About");
        $("#portalBrowseLink").text("Browse");
    };

    function setMobileStyling() {
        $(".backgroundJournalCarousel .journalCarouselText .journalCarouselTextButton").addClass("blueGrayButton mediumButton");
        $(".relatedContentHeader").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $(".articleToolsHeader").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuLink").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContentsNew").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $(".rightMobileMenuButton").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuPlaceHolder").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContents").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#rightMobileMenuLink").addClass("doNotShow");
    };

    function setTabletStyling() {
        $(".backgroundJournalCarousel .journalCarouselText .journalCarouselTextButton").removeClass("blueGrayButton mediumButton");
        $(".relatedContentHeader").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $(".articleToolsHeader").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuLink").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContentsNew").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $(".rightMobileMenuButton").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuPlaceHolder").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContents").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#rightMobileMenuLink").addClass("doNotShow");
    };

    function setDesktopStyling() {
        $(".backgroundJournalCarousel .journalCarouselText .journalCarouselTextButton").removeClass("blueGrayButton mediumButton");
        $(".relatedContentHeader").addClass("doNotShow");
        $(".articleToolsHeader").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuLink").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContentsNew").addClass("doNotShow");
        $(".rightMobileMenuButton").addClass("doNotShow");
        $("#mobileContents").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#centerMobileMenuPlaceHolder").removeClass("doNotShow");
        $("#rightMobileMenuLink").removeClass("doNotShow");
    };

    function setResponsiveLabels() {
        if (window.innerWidth < tabletBreakpoint) {
            setMobileLabels();
        } else {
            setDesktopLabels();
        }
    };

    function setResponsiveStyling() {
        if (window.innerWidth < mobileBreakpoint) {
            setMobileStyling();
        } else if (window.innerWidth < tabletBreakpoint) {
            setTabletStyling();
        } else {
            setDesktopStyling();
        }
    };

    function setMobileAccountMenu() {
        if (window.innerWidth < tabletBreakpoint) {
            $(".institutionalLoginContainer").addClass("doNotShow");
            $("#portalMobileSignIn").removeClass("doNotShow");
            $("#portalLoginBar").addClass("doNotShow");
        } else {
            $(".institutionalLoginContainer").removeClass("doNotShow");
            $("#portalMobileSignIn").addClass("doNotShow");
            $("#portalLoginBar").removeClass("doNotShow");
        }
    };
    $(document).ready(function() {
        setResponsiveLabels();
        //	setResponsiveStyling(); //Uncomment for LIT-171016 and LIT-171018
        //	setMobileAccountMenu(); //Uncomment for LIT-171021
    });
    $(window).resize(function() {
        setResponsiveLabels();
        //	setResponsiveStyling(); //Uncomment for LIT-171016 and LIT-171018 
        //	setMobileAccountMenu(); //Uncomment for LIT-171021
    });

    // Move popup author boxes within screen, if they extend further than the right border
    $(".contribDegrees").hover(function() {
        var $popUpAuthor = $(this).find(".authorLayer");
        $popUpAuthor.css({
            "left": "0px"
        });
        var xOffset = 0
        if ($(this)[0].getBoundingClientRect().height < 20) //single line
            xOffset = $(this)[0].getBoundingClientRect().left + $popUpAuthor[0].getBoundingClientRect().width - document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        else //author name extends in 2 lines
            xOffset = $(this)[0].getBoundingClientRect().right + $popUpAuthor[0].getBoundingClientRect().width - document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        if ($popUpAuthor.size() > 0) {
            if (xOffset > 0)
                $popUpAuthor.css({
                    "left": -xOffset + "px"
                });
        }
    });
</script></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="widget general-html-asset none  widget-none  widget-compact-all" id="baffaf19-0375-4434-b7e2-341584273ebb"  >
        
        

        <div class="wrapped " >
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><script type="text/javascript">

function articleToolsToggle(containerName) {
  var articleCitationID = document.getElementById('articleCitationDownloadContainer');
  var articlePermissionsID = document.getElementById('articlePermissionsContainer');
  var articleShareID = document.getElementById('articleShareContainer');
  var permissionsImageID = document.getElementById("permissionsImage");
  
  if (containerName == 'articleCitationDownloadContainer') {
	  if (articleCitationID.style.display === 'none' || articleCitationID.style.display === '') {

		articlePermissionsID.style.display = 'none';
		if (permissionsImageID) {
			permissionsImageID.src="/pb-assets/Icons/permissions-icon.png";
		}		
		
		articleShareID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("shareImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/share-icon.png";
		
		articleCitationID.style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById("citationsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/Cross.png";
		
	  } else {
		articleCitationID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("citationsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/citations-icon.png";

	  }
  } else if (containerName == 'articlePermissionsContainer') {
	  if (articlePermissionsID.style.display === 'none' || articlePermissionsID.style.display === '') {

		articleCitationID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("citationsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/citations-icon.png";

		articleShareID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("shareImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/share-icon.png";

		articlePermissionsID.style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById("permissionsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/Cross.png";
		
	  } else {
		articlePermissionsID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("permissionsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/permissions-icon.png";
	  }
  } else if (containerName == 'articleShareContainer') {
	  if (articleShareID.style.display === 'none' || articleShareID.style.display === '') {
	  
		articleCitationID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("citationsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/citations-icon.png";
		
		if (permissionsImageID) {
			permissionsImageID.src="/pb-assets/Icons/permissions-icon.png";
		}	
		
		articleShareID.style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById("shareImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/Cross.png";
		
	  } else {
		articleShareID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("shareImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/share-icon.png";
	  }
  } else {
		articleCitationID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("citationsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/citations-icon.png";

		articlePermissionsID.style.display = 'none';
		if (permissionsImageID) {
			document.getElementById("permissionsImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/permissions-icon.png";
		}
		
		articleShareID.style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById("shareImage").src="/pb-assets/Icons/share-icon.png";
  }
 };

/* Uncomment to prevent scrolling of background element, when have scrolled at the start or end of the popup
$('#articleCitationDownloadContainer').on('mousewheel', function (e){
    var event = e.originalEvent, d = event.wheelDelta || -event.detail;
    this.scrollTop += ( d < 0 ? 1 : -1 ) * 30;
    e.preventDefault();
});

$('#articleShareContainer').on('mousewheel', function(e){
    var event = e.originalEvent, d = event.wheelDelta || -event.detail;
    this.scrollTop += ( d < 0 ? 1 : -1 ) * 30;
    e.preventDefault();
});
*/

function cnpPopupToggle() {
	var cnpPopupID = document.getElementById('cnpPopup');
  
    if (cnpPopupID.style.display === 'none' || cnpPopupID.style.display === '') {
		cnpPopupID.style.display = 'block';
	} 
	else {
		cnpPopupID.style.display = 'none';
	}
  }
</script></div>
        </div>
    </div>
    



    
    
    
    
    
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
            
                
            
            
                
                
                
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
            
            
            
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
        
    
    
    

    
    <div class="widget general-html-asset none  widget-none  widget-compact-all" id="1de50480-5127-409f-a565-0dbf5ffa7816"  >
        
        

        <div class="wrapped " >
            
            <div class="widget-body body body-none  body-compact-all"><script type="text/javascript">
var mobileBreakpoint=768;
var tabletBreakpoint=1025;
function ResizeHeaderFont() {
	$('#headerTitle').css('font-size', "32px");	/*Max font size, then reduce from there*/
	$('#headerTitle h1').css('font-size', "32px");	/*Max font size, then reduce from there - journal home only*/
	var fontsize = 32;
	var headerTitleElement = document.getElementById('headerTitle');
	var headerTitleSize = headerTitleElement.getBoundingClientRect();
	var textHeight = headerTitleSize.height;
	var textWidth = headerTitleSize.width;

	var containerElement = document.getElementById('headerTitleContainer');
	var containerSize = containerElement.getBoundingClientRect();
	var containerHeight = containerSize.height;
	var containerWidth = containerSize.width;

	var fontstring = "";

	while (textHeight > containerHeight) {
		fontsize--;
		fontstring = fontsize.toString();
		fontstring = fontstring + "px";
		$('#headerTitle').css('font-size', fontstring);
		$('#headerTitle h1').css('font-size', fontstring);
		headerTitleSize = headerTitleElement.getBoundingClientRect();
		textHeight = headerTitleSize.height;
		textWidth = headerTitleSize.width;
	}
};

function isMobile() {
	var windowWidth = window.innerWidth;	
	return(windowWidth < mobileBreakpoint);
};

function stickClass(action) {
	try {
		$('.stick-it').stickIt(action);
	}
	catch(err) {
		console.log("Caught Exception in applying stick-it class: " + err.message);
	}
};

function CheckStickyResize() {
	if (isMobile()) {
		stickClass('remove');
		mobilePortalLoginSetup();
	} else {
		stickClass('add');
		portalLoginSetup();
	}
};
function SetDynamicZIndex() {
	var $stickyJournalHeader = $(".stick-it-wrapper");
	if ($stickyJournalHeader && $stickyJournalHeader.size()>0) {
		if (!isNaN(parseInt($stickyJournalHeader[0].style.height))) {
			$stickyJournalHeader.addClass("stickItZIndex");
		}
		else {
			$stickyJournalHeader.removeClass("stickItZIndex");
		}
	}
};
function CheckMobileMenu() {
	if (isMobile()) {
		$(".collapsible-container.collapsible-collapsed .collapsible-body li a").click(function () {
			closeMobileMenu('#openAccessSideMenu > ul > li > ul');
		});
	}
};
function AddItemSeparators() {
	var $ifBox = $(".impact-factor-container");
	if ($ifBox && $ifBox.size()>0) {
		$("#showAllSocietiesBtn").addClass("ifBorder");
	}
};
function CalculateExpandableModalDimensions()
{
	var $modal=$("#allSocietiesModal");
	if ($modal && $modal.size()>0) {
		var $docWidth=document.documentElement.clientWidth;
		var headerElement=$(".headerContainer")[0];
		$modal.width(headerElement.getBoundingClientRect().width);
		$modal.css({"left":"0px"}); //reset left position, in order to calculate the correct offset
		var $xOffset = $modal.offset().left-headerElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;
		if ($xOffset>0) {
			$modal.css({"left":-$xOffset+"px"});
		}
		var $blockElements = $(".headerContainer .societyLogo, .societyNameContainer");
		if ($blockElements && $blockElements.size()>0) {
			var $logoWidth = $blockElements.width();
			for (i=1; i<=5; i++) {
				var $row=$(".allPublicationPartnersContent #row"+i);
				var $societiesPerRow=$row.find('.societyImageLink');
				if ($societiesPerRow.size()>0) {
					$row.css({"margin-left": (headerElement.getBoundingClientRect().width-10-($logoWidth+2)*$societiesPerRow.size())/2+"px"});
				}
			}
		}
	}
}; 
function ShowModal() {
	$("#allSocietiesModal").css({"display":"block"});
	$("#showAllSocietiesBtn").addClass("containerSelected");
	$("#allPubPartnersBoxText > i").removeClass("arrowDown");
	$("#allPubPartnersBoxText > i").addClass("arrowUp");
	CalculateExpandableModalDimensions();
};

function HideModal() {
	$("#allSocietiesModal").css({"display":"none"});
	$("#showAllSocietiesBtn").removeClass("containerSelected");
	$("#allPubPartnersBoxText > i").removeClass("arrowUp");
	$("#allPubPartnersBoxText > i").addClass("arrowDown");
};

function SetExpandableModalBehaviour() {
	// Get the area that opens the modal
	var btn = document.getElementById("showAllSocietiesBtn");	
	if (btn) {
		// When the user clicks on the button
		btn.onclick = function() {
			if ($("#allSocietiesModal").is(":visible"))
				HideModal(); 		// if shown, hide the modal 
			else
				ShowModal(); 		// if hidden, show the modal 
		}
		// When the user presses the enter-key on the element
		btn.onkeypress = function(e) {
			if (e.keyCode === 13) { // enter key maps to keycode `13`
				if ($("#allSocietiesModal").is(":visible"))
					HideModal(); 		// if shown, hide the modal 
				else
					ShowModal(); 		// if hidden, show the modal 
			}
		}
	}
	// When the user clicks on <span> (x), close the modal
	var spanClose = document.getElementsByClassName("closeModalButton")[0];
	if (spanClose) {
		spanClose.onclick = function() { HideModal(); }
		spanClose.onkeypress = function(e) {
			if (e.keyCode === 13) { // enter key maps to keycode `13`
				HideModal();
			}
		}
	}
};

$(window).resize(function() {
	ResizeHeaderFont();
	CalculateExpandableModalDimensions();
});

$(window).scroll(function() {
	SetDynamicZIndex();
});

$(document).ready(function() {
	ResizeHeaderFont();
	CheckMobileMenu();
	AddItemSeparators();
	SetExpandableModalBehaviour();
});
</script></div>
        </div>
    </div>
